[30;1m472 | [0m[35mThe builtin Python ``subprocess.Popen`` module is great, but it can be a[0m
[30;1m473 | [0m[35mbit clunky at times. The ``os.system`` command is easy to use, but it[0m
[30;1m474 | [0m[35mdoesn't have much flexibility. The ``ub.cmd`` function aims to fix this.[0m
[30;1m475 | [0m[35mIt is as simple to run as ``os.system``, but it returns a dictionary[0m
[30;1m476 | [0m[35mcontaining the return code, standard out, standard error, and the[0m
